 aisi lut ki khud kursi hairaan he ki wo he to ek hi ab aise main is akeli kursi par itane saare netaaon ko kaise or kahaan bitha len?aisa badla khelubtan lag chukaa tha
 The baraatis were also ready
 akhabaaron main khabaren print hone ke liye chali gayi thi

 tabhi raat ke andhere main achaanak duulhaa badal gaya

 sau baaten hone lagati hai

 logon ko aise mili hairaan karne vaali khabarder tak jaagane vaali mumbai abhi subah kii agosh main thi

 jo jaage the unke hisse main shapath aa gai or jo rahe the unke hisse sirf dhokhe kii chapat ai

 soshal media par tafarih tab bhi jari thi

 or ab bhi jari he jab uddhav thakare ke netritv main shivasena, ensipi or congress sarkaar banane se chook gai thi
 The day-night game was continued with the counting of mlas on the other side
 pal-pal tasviir badal rahi thi

 pataa chalaa 104 or paanch kaa jod-ghataav shuru ho gaya

 ginati se lekar ghode or khachchar par bahes shuru ho gai

 jin vidhayakon kii ginati se maharashtra main nai sarkaar banani he

 phir kya tha hotel waalon ke daawey bhi kuch is anbaaj main aane lage
 The game of power continues but the game continues
 bas maze lijie

 sarkaar kiski banegi ye to main nahin jaanata
 But i can already say with such a claim that whichever government will come, they will say it with a very sweet tongue and with full respect that whatever we did was done by keeping the interest of the people of Maharashtra in front
 resler gita phogot ke liye ravivaar kaa din kaaphi khaas he kyonki aaj vah shaadi ke bandhan main bandhane vaali hai 
 Bollywood actor Aamir Khan made his day more special
 aamir, gita kii shaadi atend karne ke liye haryana ke bhivani pahunche the

 lekin gita ne yah lene se manaa kar diya tha

 gita bharat kii jaani-maani resler hai

 bataa den, aane vaali film 'dangal'main aamir mahavir phogot kaa hi kirdaar nibhaa rahe hai

 aamir puure phogot parivaar ke behad kareebi hai

 Was there any advice behind this decision? Nobody knows this, but there are many contenders for this, who say that on their advice, PM Modi took this bold decision
 haalanki pradhanmantri narendra modi kaaphi samay se kalaadhan ke mudde ko uthaate rahe hai or is mudde kaa istemaal karke raajnneetik pratidwandiyon par hamale bhi karte rahe hai
 In the last Lok Sabha election, this issue and the issue of corruption became very important
 is mudde ne vastav main matadaataaon ko kaaphi had tak prabhavit bhi kiya
 Now that PM Modi has attacked the black money on the lines of 'surgical strike', then there are many people who claim that PM Modi took this step after considering his advice
 maharashtra ke anil bokil naam ke ek or shakhya hai jo kalaadhan ke khilaaf kaaphi samay se muhim chalaa rahe hai
 He also claims that he met Prime Minister Narendra Modi on this issue
 is mulaakaat main unhone piem modi ko samajhaayaa tha ki kaise ek jatke main kaale dhan ke mudde par kuch samay ke liye kaabo paaya ja saktaa he
 Anil Bokil of Aurangabad, Maharashtra formed a group called Arthakranti
 ve kuch samay se 1,000 or 500 ke noton par pratibandh lagane kii maang bhi kar rahe the
 Bokil's first meeting with Prime Minister Modi was in 2012 when Modi was the Chief Minister of Gujarat
 arthkranti sanstha kaa daawa he ki bhartiya arthvyavastha main 95 pratishat hissaa 500, 1000 or 100 rupee kaa he
 While the average income of the common man of the country is only Rs 150 per month
 aise me zyada bade noton kaa prayog keval kaala dhan jamaa karne ke liye hota he
 It is helpful in creating and raising black money
 enditivi se baat karte hue anil bokil ke sahaayak arun phoke ne bataaya ki pehali baar anil bokil ne narendra modi se 2013 main mulaakaat kii thi
 This meeting took place when Modi was the Chief Minister of Gujarat and he was declared the bjp's candidate for the post of PM
 unhone daawa kiya ki bokil ke sujhaavon maanane ke baad hi sarkaar ne yah kadam uthaaya he
 Arun said that he had got only 9 minutes to meet Chief Minister Modi, but Modi's interest in the subject increased greatly and the discussion lasted more than two hours
 mukhyamantri modi ko bokil ke suzav kaaphi achche lage or unhone tab sakaaratmak jawaab diya tha
 Arun claims that even when Narendra Modi won the elections in 2014 and became PM, he met Bokil
 arun kaa kahana he ki donon ne kai baar mulaakaat kii
 This meeting was kept secret
 itnaa hi nahin arun kaa kahana he ki piem modi ne apane kai adhikariyon ke saath bokil kii mulaakaat karwaai or to or bokil ke pregentation karwaae gaye
 Bokil put his point before many economists
 tamaam jagahon se santusht hone ke baad piem modi ne iske liye taiyaari kar lee
 But the most important advice was to get people connected to the banking system
 arun kaa daawa he ki bokil ne sabase pehle isaki vyavastha karne kii baat kahi thi
 This is the reason that the accounts of poor people were opened under the first Jan Dhan Yojana
 phir is yojana ko lagu kiya gaya
 Arun said that Earth revolution has been asking the government to fulfill the five demands
 abhi sarkaar ne keval ek hi maang maani he
 Yoguru Baba Ramdev is also among the contenders
 yah to sabko pataa he ki baba ramdev kaaphi samay se kaale dhan ke khilaaf muhim chalaa rahe hai
 He is also not behind in taking credit for the government's move
 unhone ek twit share kiya he jisamen unhone bataaya he ki unhone kaaphi pehle (4 june 2011 ko) is prakaar kii baat kahi thi or sarkaar ko yah karne ke liye kaha tha
 But the Congress-led UPA government did not take this step
 vaise yah to saaf hi he ki baba ramdev pradhanmantri narendra modi ke samarthak hai

 pichley loksabhaa chunaav main yah mudda or bhrashtachar kaa mudda kaaphi ahm ho gaya

 ab jab piem modi ne kaale dhan par 'sargical strike' kii tarj par hamalaa kar diya he tab kai aise log saamne aa rahe hai jinka daawa he ki piem modi ne unki salaah par gaur karke yah kadam uthaaya
 There is another legend named Anil Bokil of Maharashtra who has been campaigning against black money for a long time
 unka bhi daawa he ki unhone is mudde par pradhanmantri narendra modi se mulaakaat kii thi

 pradhanmantri modi se bokil kii pehali mulaakaat 2012 main us samay hui thi jab modi gujarat ke mukhyamantri the
 The Economy Institute claims that 95 per cent of the Indian economy is 500, 1000 and 100 rupees
 jabaki desh ke aam aadmi kii ausat aay keval 150 rupee pratimah he

 yah kaala dhan banane or badhaane main sahaayak he

 yah mulaakaat tab hui thi jab modi gujarat ke mukhyamantri the or unhen bijepi ne apana piem pad kaa ummidavaar ghoshit kiya tha

 arun ne bataaya ki mukhyamantri modi se mulaakaat ke liye keval 9 minute kaa samay mila tha lekin vishay main modi kii ruchi bahut badi or charchaa do ghante se bhi zyada chali
 Chief Minister Modi liked Bokil's suggestions very well and had responded positively then
 arun kaa daawa he ki jab narendra modi 2014 main chunaav jite or piem bane uske baad bhi unhone bokil se mulaakaat kii
 Arun says that the two met several times
 is mulaakaat ko gupt hi rakhaa gaya

 kai arthshaastriyon ke samaksh bokil ne apni baton ko rakhaa

 lekin sabase zyada jaruri salaah yah thi ki logon ko banking vyavastha se joda jaae
 Arun claims that Bokil first talked about arranging it
 yahi vajah he ki pehle jandhan yojana ke tahat garib logon ke khate khole gaye
 The scheme was then implemented
 arun ne kaha ki arthkranti sarkaar se paanch maangon ko puraa karne kii baat kahati rahi he
 Right now the government has accepted only one demand
